<div id="review_1802099355" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1802099355" />
    <a title="Mohammed Arabey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13592557-mohammed-arabey"><img alt="Mohammed Arabey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364338486p2/13592557.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1802099355?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mohammed Arabey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mohammed Arabey" href="/user/show/13592557-mohammed-arabey">Mohammed Arabey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/22456224-the-lightning-thief">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Mohammed by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14485406-raoufa-ibrahim">Raoufa Ibrahim</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1802099355" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8590061258123108118"><b>One of the Greatest Urban Fantasy's Beginning I've ever read.</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487701465i/22042662._SX540_.jpg' width='450' height='337' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><i><br/>Now as I join Hogwarts every September to May, I'll spend my Summers in Half Blood Camps.<blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487701465i/22042663.jpg' width='300' height='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></blockquote>It's awfully late for me, I know. But I was stubborn enough to not listen to 2 of my best half blood friends here on Goodreads to visit the Olympians.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487701810ra/22042705.gif' width='450' height='189' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><b><blockquote>“Gods—the forces you call the Greek gods—are very much alive.”</blockquote></b></i><b>I can't believe it's just Mr. Rick Riordan’s first novel.<br/>And Believe me if you didn't read it..you missed a real great series..<br/><br/>Very well w</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8590061258123108118" style="display:none"><b>One of the Greatest Urban Fantasy's Beginning I've ever read.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487701465i/22042662._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="337" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><i><br>Now as I join Hogwarts every September to May, I'll spend my Summers in Half Blood Camps.<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487701465i/22042663.jpg" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote>It's awfully late for me, I know. But I was stubborn enough to not listen to 2 of my best half blood friends here on Goodreads to visit the Olympians.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487701810ra/22042705.gif" width="450" height="189" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><b><blockquote>“Gods—the forces you call the Greek gods—are very much alive.”</blockquote></b></i><b>I can't believe it's just Mr. Rick Riordan’s first novel.<br>And Believe me if you didn't read it..you missed a real great series..<br><br>Very well written, well paced, amazing bunch of characters &amp; funny sarcastic tone that you'll love no matter you're twelve or thirty three.<br><br>And creepy atmosphere and nightmarish scenes, interwoven with huge honest references of the Greek myth that serves as crazy urban fantasy theories related to our real life..<br><br>All that in a very hell of very thrilling real roller coaster plot, that takes you across the United States, and back again..<br><br>A story that serve for one complete story for 'Book One', and leaves you longing for the next ones that promising of even bigger plot.<br><br>Now, if you're still want me to talk about why you should start reading this series, heres the above's ..<br><u>ANALYSE ▪▪</u><br><br>Very Well Written.</b> (4.75)<br>-------------------<br>Smoothly you step into the character, Percy, the narrator.. His life, bits about his past, then bit by bit into the conflict(s), then the Greek Mythology … then the Quest(s)..<br>Finding the Lighting Thief... which is not as easy as it seem..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487702843i/22042827.png" width="450" height="175" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>ups and down with thriller and chilling and creepy and even funny parts. Everything smooth and well explained with what serve book one -with hints that sure will serve later books-<br><br><b>Well Paced.</b> (4.99)<br>------------<br>See above. I truly rarely felt like that with most new YAs… always there's this boring slow parts that show up every now and then.<br>here everything measured , not too heavy boring flashbacks nor prolonged scene full of rant as many action YAs... it's like the amazing Harry Potter pace if u know what I mean.<br><br><br><b>Amazing Bunch of Characters</b> (4.5) <br>--------------------------<br>I loved Percy, really. May be because everything smoothly introduced. And he just keep in character, I mean for 12 years old kid, would you believe he'd go to the dangerous underworld to retrieve the Lighting weapon from The Lighting Thief? Just because some gods will do wars for it? “Blaa-ha-ha!”.<br> Well... when you read his reason and motivation you'll find that it's more believable and true to the character.<br>And I love that.<br><br>Also having Attention Defucit Hyperactivity Disorder (ADHD) and Dyslexia as well as it served an important point of making the high fantasy of the Greek Myth into our real world-urban- fantasy, it also a good touch to encourage any kid who suffers that -which is bit more than you may think- anyone can be hero.. just don't make it stops you. Percy didn't stop trying to read the whole book.. -kinda-<blockquote>
  <i>“Or maybe they’d realized I got my essay on Tom Sawyer from the Internet without ever reading the book and now they were going to take away my grade. Or worse, they were going to make me read the book. ” </i>
</blockquote><br>Annabith also was a fun to read. So smart. Groover... also this good "strange" friend..<br>And I also loved the mother and her love of Blue food. <i>that reminds me..So long no photo, here's some blue food.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487705108i/22043056._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="337" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i><br><br>Also all the other characters are very well introduced.. just as every thing.<br><br><b>Funny Sarcastic Tone</b> (4.5)<br>--------------------<br>Very easy lines, smart, wit, not just for the young age but really for all. -unlike my previous encounter with Magnus.- It's so funny here and in the point.<br><br><b>Creepy Atmosphere and Nightmarish Scenes</b> (5)<br>---------------------------------------<br>It's not supposed to be a horror story. But it has a lot of creepy places the friends visit.. Like this "Ever after" Las Vegas Casino...or Medusa's Shop for statues.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487705108i/22043057.jpg" width="450" height="246" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And also the way Rick Riordan writes the nightmare scenes is really full of horror and creepy symbols.<br><br>And speaking of symbols ;<br><br><b>Relating Greek Myth to our Real World.</b> (5) <br>--------------------------------<br>I am NOT a fan of Fantasy, I just prefer, rather adore URBAN FANTASY<i> -Which is why I didn't like Magnus for some serious violation to the real world-</i><br>But this one really smartly written, with real references to actual myths or work of art and literature work.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487705108i/22043058._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved how Mr. Rick connect the prosperity of the ancient Greek myth and civilisation with the current American one.<br>His theory here is so smart..and convenient enough to fall in love and immerse into his well crafted world..<br><br>And if you're, like me, not feeling well about the gods concept.. he also have a convenient idea here ;<blockquote>
  <i>“Well, now,” Chiron said. “God—capital G, God. That’s a different matter altogether. We shan’t deal with the metaphysical.”<br> “Metaphysical? But you were just talking about—”<br>“Ah, gods, plural, as in, great beings that control the forces of nature and human endeavors: the immortal gods of Olympus. That’s a smaller matter.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487705108i/22043060._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="253" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So, as I said, it's the amazing blending of the myth with real life in America is what makes it an excellent Urban Fantasy..<br><br>And speaking of America.<br><b><br>A Thrilling real Roller Coaster Plot </b> (4.5)<br><b> that Takes you Across the United States</b> (4.99)<br><b> and back again..</b> <br>----------------------------------<br>Although the first story for Percy supposed to be just an "introduction" to this world, but you find yourself gotten into a hell of adventure full of crazy chase and creepy places hidden in real world..<br>There's this great concept of "the Mist", that surrounding the myth creatures among us as the story goes..<br><blockquote>
  <i>“It's funny how humans can wrap their mind around things and fit them into their version of reality.” </i>
</blockquote><br>This theme of mist repeated in a good measure to keep the illusion that it's real story happening in our real world in a real famous places along the US.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487783336i/22050885._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="302" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And I loved visiting about 3 or 4 states and important places there through the first adventure only...and I believe more is coming in this Adventure Packed series..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487705108i/22043061._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="457" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>So, finally... if you're a Harry Potter fan..or any newer YA fantasy fan... or if you're old school mythology fan, you'll love to join us the Half Blood Camp.. trust me.<br><br>A special thanks to my half blood friends who encouraged me repeatedly on starting this amazing series <i>-why you didn't push me even harder :), kidding-</i>, thanks again truly I'd never read it without your recommendation -felt I was too old to join another huge,full of books and many series.<br>but Rick Riordant really worth the read. He got his style,, may be reminded me with Harry Potter's first book structure..but wasn't it the greatest structure ever?<br>The point that he used it creating a whole new exciting crazy myth/modern adventure..<br><br><br>Mohammed Arabey<br>With the Olympians from 3 Nov. 2016<br>To 9 Nov. 2016</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/18190302-percy-jackson-and-the-lightning-thief">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36873117-mxa?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36873117-mxa?shelf=re-read-worthy">re-read-worthy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2007930803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12432599622116077701">The only word I can think of that’s relevant to how I felt about this book is <i>
  <b>Fun, Fun, Fun</b>
</i>. Why in the world haven’t I picked this book up when I was in middle school, I’ll never know. Lbr, what’s in the past is in the past and I’ll just have to get over the fact that I might have crawled out of my shy shell sooner if these books were in my life earlier. On a positive note, I have the whole series on hand ready for me to binge as well as 2763274 other series to look forward to. that’s <b>#sort</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12432599622116077701" style="display:none">The only word I can think of that’s relevant to how I felt about this book is <i>
  <b>Fun, Fun, Fun</b>
</i>. Why in the world haven’t I picked this book up when I was in middle school, I’ll never know. Lbr, what’s in the past is in the past and I’ll just have to get over the fact that I might have crawled out of my shy shell sooner if these books were in my life earlier. On a positive note, I have the whole series on hand ready for me to binge as well as 2763274 other series to look forward to. that’s <b>#sorta #winning.</b><br><br>So, I’m one of those readers (if there are even such readers) that added this to my TBR solely for its fan art because ooooooo boooiiiii. <b>!!! THE FAN ART !!!</b> aaaaand at the time, it wasn’t even my intention to purchase the boxset but I came across it for a very cheap price so me being me, I couldn’t resist it. *<i>imma also get outta my system about how time wasn’t on my side and that I waited a whole month for it to come in the mail but now I see that it’s totally worth it.</i>*<br><br>With that said, I can finally jump into my semi-coherent feels that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28187.The_Lightning_Thief__Percy_Jackson_and_the_Olympians___1_" title="The Lightning Thief (Percy Jackson and the Olympians, #1) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lightning Thief</a> have bestowed upon me:<br><br>- <b>#1 CHARACTERS</b>. Percy, Grove and Annabeth = squad goals. I love how they’re all so different from each other and would literally go to the ends of the earth <i>for</i> each other. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466353831ra/19471721.gif" width="480" height="332" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>- Just by reading the first line of the first page, I knew that this book would be packed with sarcasm. I didn’t care that it was a middle grade novel and that there may be some cliches here and there. I was all chill while my wonderful babies were out having the time of their lives, saving the world and of course trying not to get themselves killed in the meantime :’)<br><br>- I loved how the writing was simple in that I’m learning elements of mythology without all the crazy info dump that YA/NA fantasies usually have. Tbh, I don’t remember a time where mythology didn’t interest me yet I pretty much went into this knowing very little. <i>I know, I know it’s weird.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465480826ra/19362897.gif" width="500" height="231" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>- I love me some books that I can fly by, especially during a time in need aka I-found-the-cure-to-my-really-strange-reading-slump. The book is filled with hilarious banters, adventures and action and the pacing was just wonderful. <br><br>- Grover is me. <br>- I love how Annabeth loves to read.<br>- Percy is a cinnamon roll. <br><br>- Overall, I low-key want to ditch my current reads and just get to the sequel already :’)</span>
  <a data-text-id="12432599622116077701" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5715296274649980868"><br/>Who knew middle school books could make me gush and squeal like a 12-year old. I loves!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485202759i/21793136._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Can we just appreciate how much <b> FAN ART </b> there is in this fandom???!!!??? ٩(^ᴗ^)۶<br/><br/><b> <i> “If you’re reading this because you think you might be one, my advice is: close this book right now. Believe whatever lie your mom or dad told you about your birth, and try to lead a normal life. </i> </b><br/><br/>This book is informative, interesting, funny, charming, it’s just all of the above and I’m already trash. <br/><br/><i> The Lightening Thief, </i> </span>
  <span id="freeText5715296274649980868" style="display:none"><br>Who knew middle school books could make me gush and squeal like a 12-year old. I loves!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485202759i/21793136._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can we just appreciate how much <b> FAN ART </b> there is in this fandom???!!!??? ٩(^ᴗ^)۶<br><br><b> <i> “If you’re reading this because you think you might be one, my advice is: close this book right now. Due to his birthright, Percy is expected to embark on quests and save the world from impending war. <br><br>Now it’s not just Percy that’s a sweet darling child who’s sassy and brave and courageous, it’s also his comrades, Annabeth (GIMME MORE PERCABETH PELASE) and Grover, his peculiar little friend. <br>The trio of this group is so wonderfully entertaining to read about it.     <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries"><img alt="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557144778p2/15335689.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1940112653?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries">destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781484787786" href="/book/show/36382384-the-lightning-thief">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1940112653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8379106511870053080"><blockquote>#1 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1940112653' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Lightning Thief</a> ★★★★☆<br/>#2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698507' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Sea of Monsters</a> ★★★★☆<br/>#3 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698552' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Titan’s Curse</a> ★★★★☆<br/>#4 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698564' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Battle of the Labyrinth</a> ★★★★★<br/>#5 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698573' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Last Olympian</a> ★★★★★</blockquote><br/><b>“The real world is where the monsters are.”</b><br/><br/>First of all, yes, this was actually my first time reading any of Riordan's books. I know, about a decade late on this one, but this book released right as I was reaching that funny teen age where I felt like I <i>had to</i> shift away from MG, into YA, so I kind of turned my nose up at these years ago. As an adult, of</span>
  <span id="freeText8379106511870053080" style="display:none"><blockquote>#1 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1940112653" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lightning Thief</a> ★★★★☆<br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698507" rel="nofollow noopener">The Sea of Monsters</a> ★★★★☆<br />#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698552" rel="nofollow noopener">The Titan’s Curse</a> ★★★★☆<br />#4 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698564" rel="nofollow noopener">The Battle of the Labyrinth</a> ★★★★★<br />#5 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2132698573" rel="nofollow noopener">The Last Olympian</a> ★★★★★</blockquote><br /><b>“The real world is where the monsters are.”</b><br /><br />First of all, yes, this was actually my first time reading any of Riordan's books. I know, about a decade late on this one, but this book released right as I was reaching that funny teen age where I felt like I <i>had to</i> shift away from MG, into YA, so I kind of turned my nose up at these years ago. As an adult, of course, I've started coming back to my beloved middle grade books, and I knew it was about time that I started this series. <br /><br />This book was, more than anything, really <i>cute</i>. Percy is a very enjoyable narrator: he's spunky, brave, quick-witted, and sarcastic as hell, plus he has a few great friends at his side, like Grover and Annabeth. It was so fun to watch these three interact with one another, and I found myself with a particular soft spot for Grover's vague patheticness most of the time. The interactions between the kids, of course, did remind me of another brave young trio, with a spunky "chosen one" MC, a dopey and vaguely pathetic male friend, and a smart and snarky female friend... Hmm, I wonder...<br /><br />I digress. I will admit that I had to remind myself not to compare too heavily to the early Harry Potter books, because there were some definite parallels, in my opinion, but they weren't blaring enough to make me dislike the book or feel any sort of need to blame Riordan of ripping anyone off. Despite the similarities, this book did have its own special style, down to the very casual and authentic-sounding voice of Percy's narrations, which definitely reminded me of, well... talking to a preteen boy, except maybe not as annoying as those interactions often go in real life.<br /><br />The plot is fun and predictable, the humor is cute and silly, and the twists probably won't shock anyone who isn't in the book's intended age range, but none of those things take away from the fact that this was a really solid start to the series. I was especially fond of the depictions of the gods; especially cold portrayals of Charon and Hades, who have always been two of my absolute favorite Greco-Roman beings.<br /><br />All in all, it wasn't a book that made me want to binge read the entire remainder of Riordan's bibliography in one go or anything, but I did definitely enjoy it and will be picking up the rest of this series (as well as his other series, I'm sure). I'd recommend this to anyone who enjoys middle grade fantasy, and <b>especially</b> any younger teens or preteens who want something fun to read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8379106511870053080" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1962607719" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1962607719" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1962607719?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1962607719" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2972696923934010246"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1490115631ra/22283286.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> “It's funny how humans can wrap their mind around things and fit them into their version of reality.” </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>First of all: Now I see why so many people are angry at the movies. They’re so different. <br/>I mean, they have some similarities, but in a big way they’re different. <br/>And what can I say? Am I surprised that I liked the book more than the movie? <br/>No, absolutely not. <br/>I liked the movies, but after I saw what the real story should’ve been like, I think they could’ve made more of it. <br/>Sec</span>
  <span id="freeText2972696923934010246" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1490115631ra/22283286.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> “It's funny how humans can wrap their mind around things and fit them into their version of reality.” </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>First of all: Now I see why so many people are angry at the movies. They’re so different. <br>I mean, they have some similarities, but in a big way they’re different. <br>And what can I say? Am I surprised that I liked the book more than the movie? <br>No, absolutely not. <br>I liked the movies, but after I saw what the real story should’ve been like, I think they could’ve made more of it. <br>Second: There is no question if this is a book for kids or not. It definitely is. <br>It’s for children or younger adults (I could say like me, but I’m 23 and that’s probably older than a normal young adult is - right? But who cares?) <br>That’s why I’m rating it as my thirteen year old self. <br>And my thirteen year old self loved this book. It was so different, so funny and so entertaining. It was so much fun! <br>Sadly, I had a slight idea what the ending is (thanks to the movies, duh) that’s why I wasn’t as surprised of it like others would be (but I was pretty surprised how much everything was changed in the movies?!). <br>But still.. it’s a great book and I can’t wait to continue the story of Percy and his friends.<br><br>Characters ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Is my thirteen year old self in love with Percy? Probably. <br>Is she in love with Annabeth? Yep. <br>And does she wants to have a best friend like Grover ? Absolutely. <br>Sure, there could’ve been more depth and a bit more character development. But it’s a children’s book, guys. Not an adult high end fantasy. <br>So it was okay, it was good. It fitted the story perfectly and left a little bit open for the next few books.<br><br>World ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>You know what? My first Rick Riordan book were the books about Greek gods and heroes. <br>And I literally devoured them. <br>One day and I was finished with these light and funny books that taught me a little bit about Greek mythology. <br>(I tried some adult books and I got to page 3 or 4 and I was like: Nope, sorry. So dry and slow and soooooo confusing.) <br>So if you ever want some funny background (that maybe isn’t really historical correct?) of the Greek mythology and Percy’s world, then you should definitely try out these books. <br>But back to the main book: if you know just a tiny bit of the Greek mythology you know that there Is an Olympus full of gods and on earth there are humans and some rare half gods. Even though these were the stories of a time really far away, Rick Riordan is putting them back into our reality and our timeline. <br>It’s hugely entertaining and funny and I loved it, even though there could’ve been more depth to the whole world building (but maybe that’s just a first book illness and it’s getting better with every book - who knows?) <br>All in all it was really good for the genre it’s in. <br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Oh, friendship is such a huge word in this book (it’s a children’s book, remember?) and it was so heartwarming and so so cute. <br>They were so loyal to each other and always protected and fought for each other. <br>It was just so adorable and so cool. <br>If I ever had the chance to meet these guys, I would totally join the group - even as an 98,12% human (who knows - right?🤷🏻‍♀️). <br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Well, it was funny. And entertaining. <br>But it wasn’t worth five stars. <br>It was a good, nice language. Fitting for a children’s book and a light hearted but still action filled story.<br>It’s definitely worth trying it out even if you’re an adult and waited years to read it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2972696923934010246" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8IYqHGOp0cOaoSMPQDAKilVeLLvqHoIT0ZZNBZ2V6/6Bg0DfiR9P/2aBSRbYs1bHGeO6+rVNdMosG3BNDXCrLQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bgQKAtfLBN8u+YTDvFl1ld8uZoUfXDnVEGelytSS0LAfAWDBPX2a49LZ7tok2inYk5PwxEAPzwzt6piCRHeQYw==')})
  }
